.. _net.fxarena.openfx.Polaroid:

Polaroid node
=============

|pluginIcon| 

*This documentation is for version 1.4 of Polaroid.*

Description
-----------

Polaroid image effect node.

Inputs
------

+----------+---------------+------------+
| Input    | Description   | Optional   |
+==========+===============+============+
| Source   |               | No         |
+----------+---------------+------------+
| Mask     |               | Yes        |
+----------+---------------+------------+
